============================================================
-03- COMMAND-CHANGE RELICS
------------------------------------------------------------
Coin Toss:    magic   -> wombsca
DragoonBoots: sketch  -> tools
FakeMustache: saferpo -> slot
Gem Box:      item    -> runic
Thief Glove:  gprain  -> jump

============================================================
-04- COMMANDS
------------------------------------------------------------

3xElem
-------
3 times, use a random elemental skill (excluding black magic spells).
Equal chance of any of the following:
  Absolute 0, Acid Rain, Aero, Air Blade, Aqua Rake, AuraBolt, Bio Blast, Bismark, Blaze, Bolt Beam, Bolt Edge, CleanSweep, El Nino, Elf Fire, Fire Beam, Fire Dance, Fire Skean, Fire Wall, Flare Star, Gale Cut, Mega Volt, Plasma, Pois. Frog, Sand Storm, Shiva, Slide, Super Ball, Tek Laser, Tritoch, Virite, Water Edge, WaveCannon

AtomLif
-------
Use the combo Atomic Ray + Life 2.

DisRefl
-------
Use the combo Dischord + Reflect???.

R-Nuke
-------
Use a random non-elemental magic damage skill.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  7-Flush, Bahamut, Chocobop, Cokatrice, Crusader, Drain, Empowerer, Exploder, Flare, Goner, H-Bomb, Heart Burn, HyperDrive, L.4 Flare, Land Slide, Maduin, Megahit, Meteo, Osmose, Quasar, Rage, Rasp, Retort, Revenge, Shock Wave, Shrapnel, Step Mine, Stone, Stunner, Ultima, Whump, Wombat

SafeRPo
-------
Use the combo Safe + R.Polarity.

ScarIce
-------
Use the combo Scar Beam + Ice.

TraMudd
-------
Use the combo Train + Muddle.

WombSca
-------
Use the combo Wombat + Scan.
